# Layer 2 ATT&CK Base Risk Scores

Authoritative Layer 2 base score table for MITRE ATT&CK techniques.
Layer 2 uses `base_threat_score_0_10` as the lookup value, then applies banking asset criticality and independent-verification caps.
`previous_score_0_10` records the generated seed score before banking SOC recalibration.

| rank | attack_id | attack_vector | tactics | base_threat_score_0_10 | base_threat_grade | previous_score_0_10 | calibration_reason | source_impact_score | source_exploit_likelihood | exploit_likelihood_reason | severity_label | max_surface | max_edge_case | edge_case_flags | related_capec_ids | related_cwe_ids | data_sources | mitigation_ids | mitigations |
